 Today is Govardhan Puja 2018 worship
 diwalike duusare din annakut orgovardhan poojaki jaati he
 Originally it is the worship of nature, which was started by Shri Krishna
 is din prakruti ke aadhaar, parvat ke rup main govardhan kii puja kii jaati he or samaaj ke aadhaar ke rup main gaay kii puja kii jaati he
 It started from Pujabras and gradually became prevalent throughout India
 kis prakaar karen govardhan puja?- praatah kaal sharir par tel malkar snaan karen
 - Draw the shape of Govardhan with cow dung at the main entrance of the house
 - gobar kaa govardhan parvat banaaen, paas main gwaal bal,pedpaudhon kii akruti banaaen
 - Put the idol of Lord Krishna in the middle
 - iske baad bhagwan krishna, gwaal-bal,or govardhanparvatkaa shodashopchaar pujan karen
 - Offer dish and panchamrit
 - govardhan puja kii katha sunen, prasad vitaran karen or sabake saath bhojan karen
 How is Annakoot worshiped? - Varuna, Indra, Agni are worshiped on this day in the Vedas
 - saath main gaayon kaa shringaar karke unki aarti kii jaati he or unhen fal mithaiyaan khilaai jaati hai
 - a replica of Govardhan Parvat is made from cow dung
 - iske baad uski pushp, dhoop, deep , naivedhy se upasna kii jaati he
 - On this day, a heirloose meal is made for every member of the household
 - bhojan main vividh prakaar ke pakwaan banaae jate hai
 Two special uses of Govardhan Puja- 1- Remedy for getting children- Make panchamrit from milk, curd, honey, sugar and milk
 - isamen gangaajal or tulsi dal milaayein
 - Offer Lord Panchamrit by filling Lord Krishna in a conch
 - iske baad "clin krishna clin" kaa 11 maala jaap karen
 Eclipse Panchamrit, your wishes will be fulfilled
 2- aarthik sampannataa or samruddhi ke liye upaay- gaay ko snaan karakar uskaa tilak karen
 - Feed him fruit and fodder
 - gaay kii saat baar parikrama karen
 - Take the soil near the hoof of the cow
 - isekanchaki shishi main apane paas surakshit rakh len

 kya hota he louletara of anderteking (lou) ek tarah se bank guarantee hoti he

 lou jari karne vaala bank guaranter ban jaataa he or vah apane client ke lone par principal amount or us par lagane vaale byaaj ko bina shart bhugtan karnaa sweekaar karata he

 rojaanaa kii banking tranjactions ko proces karne vaale kor banking system (CBS) ko ye karmchaaree chakma de gaye
 Through this, they passed the guarantee given on the lous without the necessary approval and on the basis of this, the overseas branches of Indian banks gave loans
 SWIFT kya he?jab bhi kisi bank kii taraf se lou jari kiya jaataa he
 After this, information about credit transfer is given to the bank abroad

 sarvapalliradhakrishnanjhinake sammaan main unke janmdiwas yani 5 sitambar ko desh main shikshak diwas manaaya jaataa he
 Let's know many important things related to his life
 
 
 - dow
 Radhakrishnan was a great educationist
 unka kahana tha ki shiksha kaa matlab sirf jaankaree dena hi nahin he

 dow
 Radhakrishnan believed that unless the teacher was devoted and committed to education, education would not get the form of mission
 - apane jivan main adarsh shikshak rahe bharat ke dwitiya raashtrapati dow
 Radhakrishnan was born on 5 September 1888 in Tirutani village, Tamil Nadu
 inke pita sarvapalli veeraswami rajasav vibhaag main kaam karte the
 His mother's name was Sitamma
 inaki praarambhik shiksha lunarth mishanri skool, tirupati or vellore main hui

 1903 main yuvati sivaakamu ke saath unka vivaah hua
 Here, not 5 September, celebrates Teacher's Day on 5 October, this is the reason- Radhakrishnan studied the Bible and the philosophy of Swami Vivekananda at the age of 12
 unhone darshan shaastra se em
 a
 kiya or 1916 main madras residency college main sahaayak adhyaaapak ke taur par unki niyukti hui
 He worked as a teacher for 40 years
 - vah 1931 se 1936 tak andhra vishvavidhyalay ke kulapati rahe
 After this, he held the post of Professor at Oxford University from 1936 to 1952 and from 1939 to 1948 he was the vice-chancellor of Kashi Hindu University
 unhone bhartiya samskruti kaa gahan adhyayan kiya
 He was made the first Vice President of India in the year 1952 and was the Vice Chancellor of Delhi University from 1953 to 1962 before becoming the second President of India
 isi bich 1954 main bharat ke pratham raashtrapati dow
 Rajendra Prasad honored him with the title 'bharat Ratna'
 dow

 'and since then September 5 has been celebrated as Teachers' Day
